## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Start Validation] --> B{Check ID}
    B -->|ID is set| C[Raise ValidationError: Cannot set uuid]
    B -->|ID is null| D{Check container_type_id}
    D -->|Invalid UUID format| E[Raise ValidationError: Invalid container_type_id]
    D -->|Valid UUID| F{Check Required Fields}
    F -->|Missing fields| G[Raise ValidationError: Missing required fields]
    F -->|All present| H[Validation Success]
    C --> I[End]
    E --> I
    G --> I
    H --> I
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Test as PostContainerValidatorTest
    participant PC as PackageContainer
    participant Validator as PackageContainerValidator
    participant Error as ValidationError
    
    Test->>PC: Create instance
    Test->>PC: Set container_type_id
    Test->>PC: Set tracking_number
    Test->>PC: Set original_unit_of_measurement
    Test->>PC: Set weight
    Test->>Validator: validate(package_container, "POST")
    Validator->>Validator: Check ID is null
    Validator->>Validator: Validate container_type_id UUID
    Validator->>Validator: Check required fields
    alt Validation Fails
        Validator->>Error: Raise ValidationError
        Error-->>Test: Exception
    else Validation Succeeds
        Validator-->>Test: Success
    end
```
